# Scope: country event_target:global_event_country
acemod_crisis_manager_calculate_prethoryn_effect = {
	set_global_flag = acemod_crisis_manager_prethoryn_spawn_effect_fired
	switch = {
		trigger = end_game_years_passed
		5 < {
			break = yes
		}
		5 = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						which = acemod_crisis_manager_var_country_prethoryn_spawn_time
						value = 5
					}
				}
				set_global_flag = acemod_crisis_manager_galactic_crisis_happened
				set_global_flag = acemod_crisis_manager_prethoryn_spawned_5
				set_variable = {
					which = acemod_crisis_manager_var_country_prethoryn_spawned_year_5
					value = 5
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							is_ai = no
							is_country_type = default
						}
					}
					set_variable = {
						which = acemod_crisis_manager_var_country_prethoryn_spawned_year_5
						value = 5
					}
				}
				country_event = {
					id = crisis.10
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							has_global_flag = acemod_crisis_manager_prethoryn_spawn_skip_mtth_disabled
						}
					}
					set_global_flag = acemod_crisis_manager_prethoryn_spawn_skip_mtth_fired
					random_country = {
						limit = {
							is_country_type = default
						}
						country_event = {
							id = crisis.12
							days = 35
							random = 10
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

				set_global_flag = acemod_crisis_manager_aberrant_spawned_200
				set_variable = {
					which = acemod_crisis_manager_var_country_aberrant_spawned_year_200
					value = 200
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							is_ai = no
							is_country_type = default
						}
					}
					set_variable = {
						which = acemod_crisis_manager_var_country_aberrant_spawned_year_200
						value = 200
					}
				}
				random_country = {
					limit = {
						is_country_type = extradimensional
					}
					country_event = {
						# id = crisis.1100
						id = acemod_crisis_manager_crisis.1099						#	Use substitute cloned event as vanilla will not meet its triggers.
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

acemod_crisis_manager_calculate_contingency_effect = {
	set_global_flag = acemod_crisis_manager_contingency_spawn_effect_fired
	switch = {
		trigger = end_game_years_passed
		5 < {
			break = yes
		}
		5 = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						which = acemod_crisis_manager_var_country_contingency_spawn_time
						value = 5
					}
				}
				set_global_flag = acemod_crisis_manager_galactic_crisis_happened
				set_global_flag = acemod_crisis_manager_contingency_spawned_5
				set_variable = {
					which = acemod_crisis_manager_var_country_contingency_spawned_year_5
					value = 5
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							is_ai = no
							is_country_type = default
						}
					}
					set_variable = {
						which = acemod_crisis_manager_var_country_contingency_spawned_year_5
						value = 5
					}
				}
				country_event = {
					id = crisis.2005
				}
			}
		}
		10 = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						which = acemod_crisis_manager_var_country_contingency_spawn_time

# Reset Crisis Manager settings.
acemod_crisis_manager_reset_settings = {
	remove_global_flag = acemod_crisis_manager_active	# Disable Crisis Manager
	remove_global_flag = acemod_crisis_manager_prethoryn_spawn_skip_mtth_disabled	# Enable Fast Prethoryn Invasion Start.
	acemod_crisis_manager_reset_settings_script = yes	# For country firing menu effect.
	event_target:global_event_country = {
		acemod_crisis_manager_reset_settings_script = yes		# For global_event_country which stores actually used values.
	}
	every_country = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				is_ai = no				# For any player.
				is_country_type = default				# For any other empire players might switch to.
			}
		}
	}
}

acemod_crisis_manager_reset_settings_script = {
	set_variable = {
		which = acemod_crisis_manager_var_country_spawn_time_variable		# Change years variable.
		value = 5
	}
	set_variable = {
		which = acemod_crisis_manager_var_country_prethoryn_spawn_time		# Prethoryn spawn.
		value = 0
	}
	set_variable = {
		which = acemod_crisis_manager_var_country_contingency_spawn_time		# Contingency spawn
		value = 0
	}
	set_variable = {
		which = acemod_crisis_manager_var_country_extradimensional_spawn_time		# Extradimensional spawn
		value = 0
	}
	set_variable = {
		which = acemod_crisis_manager_var_country_aberrant_spawn_time		# Aberrant spawn
		value = 0
	}
	set_variable = {
		which = acemod_crisis_manager_var_country_vehement_spawn_time		#  Vehement spawn
		value = 0
	}
	set_variable = {
		which = acemod_var_country_acemod_lib_army_strength_modifier		# Default, use crisis strength.
		value = 0
	}
}
